\hypertarget{group___d_r_i_v_e_r_s}{}\doxysection{Sensor Driver Layer}
\label{group___d_r_i_v_e_r_s}\index{Sensor Driver Layer@{Sensor Driver Layer}}

\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Initialize hardware. Initial configuration\+:~\newline
Gyro FSR\+: +/-\/ 2000DPS~\newline
Accel FSR +/-\/ 2G~\newline
DLPF\+: 42Hz~\newline
FIFO rate\+: 50Hz~\newline
Clock source\+: Gyro PLL~\newline
FIFO\+: Disabled.~\newline
Data ready interrupt\+: Disabled, active low, unlatched. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
int \mbox{\hyperlink{group___d_r_i_v_e_r_s_ga3a4fea75686ab7d2e68634e81ccac04c}{mpu\+\_\+lp\+\_\+accel\+\_\+mode}} (unsigned char rate)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Enter low-\/power accel-\/only mode. In low-\/power accel mode, the chip goes to sleep and only wakes up to sample the accelerometer at one of the following frequencies\+: ~\newline
 MPU6050\+: 1.\+25\+Hz, 5Hz, 20Hz, 40Hz ~\newline
 MPU6500\+: 1.\+25\+Hz, 2.\+5\+Hz, 5Hz, 10Hz, 20Hz, 40Hz, 80Hz, 160Hz, 320Hz, 640Hz ~\newline
 If the requested rate is not one listed above, the device will be set to the next highest rate. Requesting a rate above the maximum supported frequency will result in an error. ~\newline
 To select a fractional wake-\/up frequency, round down the value passed to {\itshape rate}. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item

int \mbox{\hyperlink{group___d_r_i_v_e_r_s_ga02db5f25359abe84be002c543cdc3803}{dmp\+\_\+read\+\_\+fifo}} (short $\ast$gyro, short $\ast$accel, long $\ast$quat, unsigned long $\ast$timestamp, short $\ast$sensors, unsigned char $\ast$more)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Get one packet from the FIFO. If {\itshape sensors} does not contain a particular sensor, disregard the data returned to that pointer. ~\newline
 {\itshape sensors} can contain a combination of the following flags\+: ~\newline
 INV\+\_\+\+X\+\_\+\+GYRO, INV\+\_\+\+Y\+\_\+\+GYRO, INV\+\_\+\+Z\+\_\+\+GYRO ~\newline
 INV\+\_\+\+XYZ\+\_\+\+GYRO ~\newline
 INV\+\_\+\+XYZ\+\_\+\+ACCEL ~\newline
 INV\+\_\+\+WXYZ\+\_\+\+QUAT ~\newline
 If the FIFO has no new data, {\itshape sensors} will be zero. ~\newline
 If the FIFO is disabled, {\itshape sensors} will be zero and this function will return a non-\/zero error code. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item

\index{Sensor Driver Layer@{Sensor Driver Layer}!dmp\_enable\_feature@{dmp\_enable\_feature}}
\index{dmp\_enable\_feature@{dmp\_enable\_feature}!Sensor Driver Layer@{Sensor Driver Layer}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{dmp\_enable\_feature()}{dmp\_enable\_feature()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int dmp\+\_\+enable\+\_\+feature (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{unsigned short}]{mask }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Enable DMP features. The following \#define\textquotesingle{}s are used in the input mask\+: ~\newline
 DMP\+\_\+\+FEATURE\+\_\+\+TAP ~\newline
 DMP\+\_\+\+FEATURE\+\_\+\+ANDROID\+\_\+\+ORIENT ~\newline
 DMP\+\_\+\+FEATURE\+\_\+\+LP\+\_\+\+QUAT ~\newline
 DMP\+\_\+\+FEATURE\+\_\+6\+X\+\_\+\+LP\+\_\+\+QUAT ~\newline
 DMP\+\_\+\+FEATURE\+\_\+\+GYRO\+\_\+\+CAL ~\newline
 DMP\+\_\+\+FEATURE\+\_\+\+SEND\+\_\+\+RAW\+\_\+\+ACCEL ~\newline
 DMP\+\_\+\+FEATURE\+\_\+\+SEND\+\_\+\+RAW\+\_\+\+GYRO ~\newline
 NOTE\+: DMP\+\_\+\+FEATURE\+\_\+\+LP\+\_\+\+QUAT and DMP\+\_\+\+FEATURE\+\_\+6\+X\+\_\+\+LP\+\_\+\+QUAT are mutually exclusive. ~\newline
 NOTE\+: DMP\+\_\+\+FEATURE\+\_\+\+SEND\+\_\+\+RAW\+\_\+\+GYRO and DMP\+\_\+\+FEATURE\+\_\+\+SEND\+\_\+\+CAL\+\_\+\+GYRO are also mutually exclusive. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em mask} & Mask of features to enable. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
0 if successful. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{group___d_r_i_v_e_r_s_ga653ebcec6758f006dd89939e8f3c6ebb}\label{group___d_r_i_v_e_r_s_ga653ebcec6758f006dd89939e8f3c6ebb}} 
\index{Sensor Driver Layer@{Sensor Driver Layer}!dmp\_enable\_gyro\_cal@{dmp\_enable\_gyro\_cal}}
\index{dmp\_enable\_gyro\_cal@{dmp\_enable\_gyro\_cal}!Sensor Driver Layer@{Sensor Driver Layer}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{dmp\_enable\_gyro\_cal()}{dmp\_enable\_gyro\_cal()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int dmp\+\_\+enable\+\_\+gyro\+\_\+cal (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{unsigned char}]{enable }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Calibrate the gyro data in the DMP. After eight seconds of no motion, the DMP will compute gyro biases and subtract them from the quaternion output. If {\itshape dmp\+\_\+enable\+\_\+feature} is called with {\itshape DMP\+\_\+\+FEATURE\+\_\+\+SEND\+\_\+\+CAL\+\_\+\+GYRO}, the biases will also be subtracted from the gyro output. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em enable} & 1 to enable gyro calibration. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
0 if successful. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{group___d_r_i_v_e_r_s_ga02db5f25359abe84be002c543cdc3803}\label{group___d_r_i_v_e_r_s_ga02db5f25359abe84be002c543cdc3803}} 
\index{Sensor Driver Layer@{Sensor Driver Layer}!dmp\_read\_fifo@{dmp\_read\_fifo}}
\index{dmp\_read\_fifo@{dmp\_read\_fifo}!Sensor Driver Layer@{Sensor Driver Layer}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{dmp\_read\_fifo()}{dmp\_read\_fifo()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int dmp\+\_\+read\+\_\+fifo (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{short $\ast$}]{gyro,  }\item[{short $\ast$}]{accel,  }\item[{long $\ast$}]{quat,  }\item[{unsigned long $\ast$}]{timestamp,  }\item[{short $\ast$}]{sensors,  }\item[{unsigned char $\ast$}]{more }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get one packet from the FIFO. If {\itshape sensors} does not contain a particular sensor, disregard the data returned to that pointer. ~\newline
 {\itshape sensors} can contain a combination of the following flags\+: ~\newline
 INV\+\_\+\+X\+\_\+\+GYRO, INV\+\_\+\+Y\+\_\+\+GYRO, INV\+\_\+\+Z\+\_\+\+GYRO ~\newline
 INV\+\_\+\+XYZ\+\_\+\+GYRO ~\newline
 INV\+\_\+\+XYZ\+\_\+\+ACCEL ~\newline
 INV\+\_\+\+WXYZ\+\_\+\+QUAT ~\newline
 If the FIFO has no new data, {\itshape sensors} will be zero. ~\newline
 If the FIFO is disabled, {\itshape sensors} will be zero and this function will return a non-\/zero error code. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em gyro} & Gyro data in hardware units. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em accel} & Accel data in hardware units. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em quat} & 3-\/axis quaternion data in hardware units. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em timestamp} & Timestamp in milliseconds. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em sensors} & Mask of sensors read from FIFO. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em more} & Number of remaining packets. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
0 if successful. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily int dmp\+\_\+set\+\_\+gyro\+\_\+bias (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{long $\ast$}]{bias }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Push gyro biases to the DMP. Because the gyro integration is handled in the DMP, any gyro biases calculated by the MPL should be pushed down to DMP memory to remove 3-\/axis quaternion drift. ~\newline
 NOTE\+: If the DMP-\/based gyro calibration is enabled, the DMP will overwrite the biases written to this location once a new one is computed. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}

\end{DoxyParams}

Set shake rejection time. Sets the length of time that the gyro must be outside of the threshold set by {\itshape gyro\+\_\+set\+\_\+shake\+\_\+reject\+\_\+thresh} before taps are rejected. A mandatory 60 ms is added to this parameter.

\end{DoxyParams}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{group___d_r_i_v_e_r_s_ga3a4fea75686ab7d2e68634e81ccac04c}\label{group___d_r_i_v_e_r_s_ga3a4fea75686ab7d2e68634e81ccac04c}} 
\index{Sensor Driver Layer@{Sensor Driver Layer}!mpu\_lp\_accel\_mode@{mpu\_lp\_accel\_mode}}
\index{mpu\_lp\_accel\_mode@{mpu\_lp\_accel\_mode}!Sensor Driver Layer@{Sensor Driver Layer}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mpu\_lp\_accel\_mode()}{mpu\_lp\_accel\_mode()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int mpu\+\_\+lp\+\_\+accel\+\_\+mode (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{unsigned char}]{rate }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Enter low-\/power accel-\/only mode. In low-\/power accel mode, the chip goes to sleep and only wakes up to sample the accelerometer at one of the following frequencies\+: ~\newline
 MPU6050\+: 1.\+25\+Hz, 5Hz, 20Hz, 40Hz ~\newline
 MPU6500\+: 1.\+25\+Hz, 2.\+5\+Hz, 5Hz, 10Hz, 20Hz, 40Hz, 80Hz, 160Hz, 320Hz, 640Hz ~\newline
 If the requested rate is not one listed above, the device will be set to the next highest rate. Requesting a rate above the maximum supported frequency will result in an error. ~\newline
 To select a fractional wake-\/up frequency, round down the value passed to {\itshape rate}. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em rate} & Minimum sampling rate, or zero to disable LP accel mode. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
0 if successful. 
\end{DoxyReturn}


在文件 \mbox{\hyperlink{inv__mpu_8c_source}{inv\+\_\+mpu.\+c}} 第 \mbox{\hyperlink{inv__mpu_8c_source_l00888}{888}} 行定义.

函数调用图\+:

\begin{center}

\begin{figure}[H]
\begin{center}

\includegraphics[width=350pt]{group___d_r_i_v_e_r_s_ga3a4fea75686ab7d2e68634e81ccac04c_icgraph}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{group___d_r_i_v_e_r_s_ga7d0b3259346898ccd1ba6ef78bf7df97}\label{group___d_r_i_v_e_r_s_ga7d0b3259346898ccd1ba6ef78bf7df97}} 
\index{Sensor Driver Layer@{Sensor Driver Layer}!mpu\_lp\_motion\_interrupt@{mpu\_lp\_motion\_interrupt}}
\index{mpu\_lp\_motion\_interrupt@{mpu\_lp\_motion\_interrupt}!Sensor Driver Layer@{Sensor Driver Layer}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mpu\_lp\_motion\_interrupt()}{mpu\_lp\_motion\_interrupt()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int mpu\+\_\+lp\+\_\+motion\+\_\+interrupt (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{unsigned short}]{thresh,  }\item[{unsigned char}]{time,  }\item[{unsigned char}]{lpa\+\_\+freq }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Enters LP accel motion interrupt mode. The behavior of this feature is very different between the MPU6050 and the MPU6500. Each chip\textquotesingle{}s version of this feature is explained below. 

~\newline
 MPU6050\+: ~\newline
 When this mode is first enabled, the hardware captures a single accel sample, and subsequent samples are compared with this one to determine if the device is in motion. Therefore, whenever this \char`\"{}locked\char`\"{} sample needs to be changed, this function must be called again.

~\newline
 The hardware motion threshold can be between 32mg and 8160mg in 32mg increments.

~\newline
 Low-\/power accel mode supports the following frequencies\+: ~\newline
 1.\+25\+Hz, 5Hz, 20Hz, 40Hz

~\newline
 MPU6500\+: ~\newline
 Unlike the MPU6050 version, the hardware does not \char`\"{}lock in\char`\"{} a reference sample. The hardware monitors the accel data and detects any large change over a short period of time.

~\newline
 The hardware motion threshold can be between 4mg and 1020mg in 4mg increments.

~\newline
 MPU6500 Low-\/power accel mode supports the following frequencies\+: ~\newline
 1.\+25\+Hz, 2.\+5\+Hz, 5Hz, 10Hz, 20Hz, 40Hz, 80Hz, 160Hz, 320Hz, 640Hz

~\newline
~\newline
 NOTES\+: ~\newline
 The driver will round down {\itshape thresh} to the nearest supported value if an unsupported threshold is selected. ~\newline
 To select a fractional wake-\/up frequency, round down the value passed to {\itshape lpa\+\_\+freq}. ~\newline
 The MPU6500 does not support a delay parameter. If this function is used for the MPU6500, the value passed to {\itshape time} will be ignored. ~\newline
 To disable this mode, set {\itshape lpa\+\_\+freq} to zero. The driver will restore the previous configuration.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em thresh} & Motion threshold in mg. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em time} & Duration in milliseconds that the accel data must exceed {\itshape thresh} before motion is reported. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em lpa\+\_\+freq} & Minimum sampling rate, or zero to disable. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
0 if successful. 
\end{DoxyReturn}


在文件 \mbox{\hyperlink{inv__mpu_8c_source}{inv\+\_\+mpu.\+c}} 第 \mbox{\hyperlink{inv__mpu_8c_source_l02642}{2642}} 行定义.

函数调用图\+:
\nopagebreak

\begin{center}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{group___d_r_i_v_e_r_s_ga2da20453aafbbba4a0f6fb9fbdd25572}\label{group___d_r_i_v_e_r_s_ga2da20453aafbbba4a0f6fb9fbdd25572}} 
\index{Sensor Driver Layer@{Sensor Driver Layer}!mpu\_read\_fifo@{mpu\_read\_fifo}}
\index{mpu\_read\_fifo@{mpu\_read\_fifo}!Sensor Driver Layer@{Sensor Driver Layer}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mpu\_read\_fifo()}{mpu\_read\_fifo()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int mpu\+\_\+read\+\_\+fifo (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{short $\ast$}]{gyro,  }\item[{short $\ast$}]{accel,  }\item[{unsigned long $\ast$}]{timestamp,  }\item[{unsigned char $\ast$}]{sensors,  }\item[{unsigned char $\ast$}]{more }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get one packet from the FIFO. If {\itshape sensors} does not contain a particular sensor, disregard the data returned to that pointer. ~\newline
 {\itshape sensors} can contain a combination of the following flags\+: ~\newline
 INV\+\_\+\+X\+\_\+\+GYRO, INV\+\_\+\+Y\+\_\+\+GYRO, INV\+\_\+\+Z\+\_\+\+GYRO ~\newline
 INV\+\_\+\+XYZ\+\_\+\+GYRO ~\newline
 INV\+\_\+\+XYZ\+\_\+\+ACCEL ~\newline
 If the FIFO has no new data, {\itshape sensors} will be zero. ~\newline
 If the FIFO is disabled, {\itshape sensors} will be zero and this function will return a non-\/zero error code. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em gyro} & Gyro data in hardware units. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em accel} & Accel data in hardware units. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em timestamp} & Timestamp in milliseconds. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em sensors} & Mask of sensors read from FIFO. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em more} & Number of remaining packets. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
0 if successful. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{group___d_r_i_v_e_r_s_ga3773dc98eb1ba15da0091ae75abcf62f}\label{group___d_r_i_v_e_r_s_ga3773dc98eb1ba15da0091ae75abcf62f}} 
\index{Sensor Driver Layer@{Sensor Driver Layer}!mpu\_run\_self\_test@{mpu\_run\_self\_test}}
\index{mpu\_run\_self\_test@{mpu\_run\_self\_test}!Sensor Driver Layer@{Sensor Driver Layer}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mpu\_run\_self\_test()}{mpu\_run\_self\_test()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int mpu\+\_\+run\+\_\+self\+\_\+test (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{long $\ast$}]{gyro,  }\item[{long $\ast$}]{accel }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Trigger gyro/accel/compass self-\/test. On success/error, the self-\/test returns a mask representing the sensor(s) that failed. For each bit, a one (1) represents a \char`\"{}pass\char`\"{} case; conversely, a zero (0) indicates a failure. 

~\newline
 The mask is defined as follows\+: ~\newline
 Bit 0\+: Gyro. ~\newline
 Bit 1\+: Accel. ~\newline
 Bit 2\+: Compass.

~\newline
 Currently, the hardware self-\/test is unsupported for MPU6500. However, this function can still be used to obtain the accel and gyro biases.

~\newline
 This function must be called with the device either face-\/up or face-\/down (z-\/axis is parallel to gravity). 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em gyro} & Gyro biases in q16 format. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em accel} & Accel biases (if applicable) in q16 format. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
Result mask (see above). 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{Sensor Driver Layer@{Sensor Driver Layer}!mpu\_set\_compass\_sample\_rate@{mpu\_set\_compass\_sample\_rate}}
\index{mpu\_set\_compass\_sample\_rate@{mpu\_set\_compass\_sample\_rate}!Sensor Driver Layer@{Sensor Driver Layer}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mpu\_set\_compass\_sample\_rate()}{mpu\_set\_compass\_sample\_rate()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int mpu\+\_\+set\+\_\+compass\+\_\+sample\+\_\+rate (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{unsigned short}]{rate }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set compass sampling rate. The compass on the auxiliary I2C bus is read by the MPU hardware at a maximum of 100Hz. The actual rate can be set to a fraction of the gyro sampling rate. 

~\newline
 WARNING\+: The new rate may be different than what was requested. Call mpu\+\_\+get\+\_\+compass\+\_\+sample\+\_\+rate to check the actual setting. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em rate} & Desired compass sampling rate (Hz). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
0 if successful. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{Sensor Driver Layer@{Sensor Driver Layer}!mpu\_write\_mem@{mpu\_write\_mem}}
\index{mpu\_write\_mem@{mpu\_write\_mem}!Sensor Driver Layer@{Sensor Driver Layer}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mpu\_write\_mem()}{mpu\_write\_mem()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int mpu\+\_\+write\+\_\+mem (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{unsigned short}]{mem\+\_\+addr,  }\item[{unsigned short}]{length,  }\item[{unsigned char $\ast$}]{data }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Write to the DMP memory. This function prevents I2C writes past the bank boundaries. The DMP memory is only accessible when the chip is awake. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{参数}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em mem\+\_\+addr} & Memory location (bank \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} 8 $\vert$ start address) \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em length} & Number of bytes to write. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em data} & Bytes to write to memory. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
